Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    GoTo 9999:
End If
Application.EnableEvents = False


If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If


Dim CurrentColumnCount As Long

' Get the current number of columns
CurrentColumnCount = Me.Columns.count

' Check if the number of columns has increased
If CurrentColumnCount > LastColumnCount Or IsEmpty(LastColumnCount) = True Then
    LastColumnCount = CurrentColumnCount

End If

' Already Approved
If (Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WIPLevel1" Or Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WIPLevel2") And Sheet2.Range("InitAppr").Value = "Y" Then
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Initial Approval must be set to No before changes can be made", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If

' Marked Ops Done
If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDone")).Value = "P" And Sheet2.Range("GAAPView").Value = "N" Then
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Uncheck the Done Checkbox to make changes", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If

' Marked GAAP Done
If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLGAAPDone")).Value = "P" Then
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Uncheck the Done GAAP Checkbox to make changes", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If


' Check for Changed Parameters
'If Sheet2.Range("PullNewData").Value = "Y" And FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Parameters")) = "No" Then
'    MsgBox "Parameters have Changed!  Get Data from Vista", vbInformation
'    GoTo 99
'End If

'If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Parameters")) = "Yes" Then
'    Sheet2.Range("PullNewData").Value = "Y"
'End If

' Done, GAAP Done, Close
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Done")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("DoneGAAP")) = "Yes" _
    Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Close")) = "Yes" Then
    
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    Application.Undo
    
    MsgBox "Double Click to Change Value", vbInformation
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

    GoTo 99
End If


11:


Me.Unprotect "password"
'Dept
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Dept")) = "Yes" Then
    MsgBox "You can only change this field with a Lookup.  Use F4 to open List", vbInformation, "Use F4"
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    GoTo 99
End If




If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then

    Dim row As Integer
    
    ' Final Approval Yes Button
    If Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
    
        If FindIntersect(Target, Me.Range("SummaryDataInput")) = "Yes" Then
                
            If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZContractStatus") & Target.row).Value = 1 Or Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJobNumber") & Target.row).Value = "" Then
                
                ' Revenue
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProj") Then
                    Dim ORPC As Integer
                    ORPC = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProj")
                    If JTDProfitCheck(Me, ORPC, Target.Value, Target.row) = False Then
                        MsgBox "Your Entry has caused JTD Profit to Exceed Profit at Completion", vbInformation
                        Application.Undo
                        GoTo 99
                    End If
                
                
                    ' GAAP View On
                    If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn Then
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOR") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
                    Else
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
                        
                    End If
                                        
                    ' Orange
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    GoTo FormatDoneField
                    
                End If
                
                ' Cost
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProj") Then
                
                    If JTDProfitCheck(Me, Target.Column, Target.Value, Target.row) = False Then
                        MsgBox "Your Entry has caused JTD Profit to Exceed Profit at Completion", vbInformation
                        Application.Undo
                        GoTo 99
                    End If

                    If Target.Value < Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDCost") & Target.row).Value Then
                        MsgBox "Your Entry has Caused % Complete over 100%", vbInformation
                        Application.Undo
                        GoTo 99
                    End If

                    
                    
                    ' GAAP View On
                    If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn Then
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOP") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPCostNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPCostNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
                    Else
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
                        
                        
                    End If
                    ' Orange
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    GoTo FormatDoneField
                    
                End If
                
                ' Revenue Notes
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes") Then
                    ' GAAP View On
                    If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn Then
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOR") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                    Else
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                    End If
                    
                    Target.Offset(0, 1).Value = "+"
                    Target.Offset(0, 1).Font.Bold = True
                    Target.WrapText = True
                    GoTo FormatDoneField
                    
                End If
                
                
                ' Cost Notes
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes") Then
                    ' GAAP View On
                    If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn Then
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPCostNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOP") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    Else
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                    End If
                    
                    Target.Offset(0, 1).Value = "+"
                    Target.Offset(0, 1).Font.Bold = True
                    Target.WrapText = True
                    GoTo FormatDoneField
                    
                End If
                
                ' Bonus Profit
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfit") Then
                                        
                    If Target.Value > Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLProjProfit") & Target.row).Value Then
                        MsgBox "Profit Not Allowed to be More Than Profit @ Completion", vbInformation
                        Application.Undo
                        GoTo 99
                    End If
                GoTo FormatDoneField
                End If
                
                
                ' Bonus Profit Notes
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes") Then
                                        
                    Target.Offset(0, 1).Value = "+"
                    Target.Offset(0, 1).Font.Bold = True
                    Target.WrapText = True
                    Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                End If
                
                
                ' Estimator, PM, Completion Date, COLJTDBonusProfit, COLJTDBonusProfitNotes
                If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLPrjMngr") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCompDate") Or _
                    Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLNotes") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfit") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes") Then
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        ' Add Border to Done field to indicate data needs to be sent back to Vista
                        GoTo FormatDoneField
                    
                End If
                    
            
            Else
                
                Application.Undo
                
                MsgBox ("You cannot edit closed Jobs")
                
            End If
            
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZUserName") & Target.row).Value = Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value
            
        End If
        
        row = Target.row
        
        
    Else
    
        MsgBox "Month has Been Final Approved", vbInformation, "Contact Accounting"
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        Application.Undo
        Application.EnableEvents = True
    
    
    End If
    
    
Else
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input", vbInformation
    Application.EnableEvents = True

End If

GoTo 9998
FormatDoneField:
' Add Border to Done field to indicate data needs to be sent back to Vista
Dim Col As String

If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn Then
    ' GAAP View
    Col = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLGAAPDone")
Else
    ' Ops View
    Col = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDone")

End If

With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With
With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeTop)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With
With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With
With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeRight)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With

9998:

    
GoTo 10000
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an error in the Worksheet_Change Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
10000:
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

99:
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
9999:

End Sub

VBA MACRO Sheet14.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet14'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Private Sub Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick(ByVal Target As Range, Cancel As Boolean)
If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    GoTo 9999:
End If
    
If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If
' JTD Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("JTDHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("JTDPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = False
        'Me.Columns(NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("JTDHeading").Select
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Select
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "J T D"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If


' APY Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("APYHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("APYPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("APYHeading").Select
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Select
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "A P Y"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If


' CY Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("CYHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("CYPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("CYHeading").Select
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Select
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "C Y"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If

' B Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("BHeading").Select
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("BPlus").Select
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "B L"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If



' ALL Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("ALLPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+" Then
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = False
        
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = True
        
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "J T D"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "A P Y"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "C Y"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "B L"
    
    
    End If
    Me.Range("AllPlus").Select
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If








If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then
    
    'ProtectUnProtect ("Off")
    Me.Unprotect "password"
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
        
    
    ' Done
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Done")) = "Yes" Then
       If Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
            Application.EnableEvents = False
            Application.ScreenUpdating = Fales
            Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
            
            If Target.Value = "P" Then
                Target.Value = ""
                Sheet15.Range(LetDict("Sheet15")("COLDone") & Target.row).Value = ""
                Target.ClearComments
            Else
                Target.Value = "P"
                Sheet15.Range(LetDict("Sheet15")("COLDone") & Target.row).Value = "P"
            End If
            
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZUserName") & Target.row).Value = Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value
            
            UpdateRowJV Target.row, Me
            
            
            
            ' Set Border to Thin
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeTop)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeRight)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
        
            
            Application.EnableEvents = True
            Application.ScreenUpdating = True
            Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
            
        Else
    
            MsgBox "Cannot Update - Has been Final Approved For Ops", vbInformation
    
        End If
    GoTo 99
        
    End If
    
    ' JV JTD Earned Revenue
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Range("JVJTDEarnedRevenue")) = "Yes" Then
        
        Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
        
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) <> "=" Then
        
            With Selection.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
            
            Target.Formula = "=IF(" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj") & Target.row & "<>0,IF((" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDCost") & Target.row _
            & "/" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj") & Target.row & ")>0.1,(" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDCost") & Target.row & "/" & _
            LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj") & Target.row & ")*" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrRevProj") & Target.row & ",0),0)"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER") & Target.row).Value = "R"

        Else

            If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER2") & Target.row).Value <> 0 Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER2") & Target.row).Value
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg") & Target.row).Value = ""
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            End If

        End If
            
        Target.Select
        Cancel = True
      
    End If
    

    
    If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = True Then
        Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
    End If

    Application.EnableEvents = True

Else
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input!", vbInformation
End If

99:
9999:

End Sub


Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    GoTo 9999:
End If

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If

Me.Unprotect "password"

If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then

    ' Marked Ops Done
    If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDone")).Value = "P" Then
        Application.Undo
        MsgBox "Uncheck the Done Checkbox to make changes", vbInformation
        GoTo 99
    End If
    
    
    
    ' Final Approval Yes Button
    If Sheet7.Shapes("Option Button 12").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
    
        If Target.row >= 9 And Target.row <= 40 And Target.Column < 47 Then
                
            If Me.Range("A" & Target.row).Value <> "" Then
                
                ' ACCT - Final Approval (No)
                If Sheet7.Shapes("Option Button 12").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
                    
                    Sheet2.Unprotect "password"
                    Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
                            
                End If
                
                ' JV JTD Earned Revenue
                If Target.Column = COLJVGJTDEarnedRev Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                ' Ops JTD Earned Revenue
                If Target.Column = 17 Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                ' Ops JTD Cost
                If Target.Column = 18 Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDCost & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                               
                
                ' Other Columns
                If Target.Column = COLJVCurContAmt Or Target.Column = COLJVOvrRevProj Or Target.Column = COLJVOvrCostProj _
                Or Target.Column = COLJVCompDate Or Target.Column = COLJVOJTDBonusProfit Or Target.Column = COLJVGDist _
                Or Target.Column = COLJVBILLBillings Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                End If
                
                
                
            
           End If
            
        End If
     
    
        
    Else
    
        MsgBox "Month has Been Final Approved", vbInformation, "Contact Accounting"
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        Application.Undo
        Application.EnableEvents = True
    
    
    End If
    
    
Else
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input", vbInformation
    Application.EnableEvents = True

End If


    
GoTo 10000
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an automation error")

10000:
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If

99:
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic

9999:


End Sub

VBA MACRO Sheet2.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet2'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
Application.EnableEvents = False


If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("ProtectSheet")) = "Yes" Then

    If Target.Value = True Then
        ProtectUnProtect ("On")
    Else
        ProtectUnProtect ("Off")
    End If
    
End If
Application.EnableEvents = True

errexit:
End Sub
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
VBA MACRO SetColumnRanges.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/SetColumnRanges'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Option Explicit
Public NumDict As Object ' Outer dictionary: SheetCodeName -> Inner Dictionary (ColumnName -> ColumnNumber)
Public LetDict As Object ' Outer dictionary: SheetCodeName -> Inner Dictionary (ColumnName -> ColumnLetter)

Public Sub InitCols()
Set NumDict = Nothing
Set LetDict = Nothing

If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If

Call WriteDictionaryToSheet

End Sub



Sub InitializeColumnDictionaries(NumDict As Object, LetDict As Object, rowNum As Long)
    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    ' Validate row number
    If rowNum < 1 Or rowNum > 1048576 Then
        MsgBox "Error: Invalid row number. Must be between 1 and 1048576.", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Define the list of desired CodeNames
    Dim tempList As Object
    Set tempList = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    ' Add desired CodeNames (adjust as needed)
    tempList.Add "Sheet11", True
    tempList.Add "Sheet12", True
    tempList.Add "Sheet13", True
    tempList.Add "Sheet14", True
    tempList.Add "Sheet15", True
    tempList.Add "Sheet16", True
    
    
    ' Collect matching worksheets
    Dim worksheets() As Worksheet
    Dim validCount As Long
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    validCount = 0
    
    ' First pass: count valid worksheets
    For Each ws In ThisWorkbook.worksheets
        If tempList.Exists(ws.CodeName) Then
            validCount = validCount + 1
        End If
    Next ws
    
    ' Check if any valid worksheets were found
    If validCount = 0 Then
        MsgBox "Error: No worksheets with specified CodeNames found.", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Allocate array and populate with matching worksheets
    ReDim worksheets(0 To validCount - 1)
    Dim i As Long
    i = 0
    For Each ws In ThisWorkbook.worksheets
        If tempList.Exists(ws.CodeName) Then
            Set worksheets(i) = ws
            i = i + 1
        End If
    Next ws
    
    ' Validate worksheet list
    If IsEmpty(worksheets) Or Not IsArray(worksheets) Then
        MsgBox "Error: Worksheet list is empty or invalid.", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Initialize outer dictionaries
    If NumDict Is Nothing Then
        Set NumDict = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
        Set LetDict = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
    End If
    
    Dim initializedCount As Long
    initializedCount = 0
    
    ' Process each worksheet
    Dim wsVar As Variant ' Use Variant for For Each over array
    For Each wsVar In worksheets
        If wsVar Is Nothing Then
            MsgBox "Warning: Invalid worksheet in list.", vbExclamation
            GoTo NextSheet
        End If
        
        ' Cast to Worksheet
        Set ws = wsVar
        
        ' Create inner dictionaries
        Dim innerNumDict As Object
        Dim innerLetDict As Object
        Set innerNumDict = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
        Set innerLetDict = CreateObject("Scripting.Dictionary")
        
        Dim nm As Name
        Dim rng As Range
        Dim colNum As Long
        Dim colLetter As String
        Dim count As Long
        Dim localName As String
        
        
        count = 0
        ' Process sheet-scoped names
        For Each nm In ws.Names
            On Error Resume Next
            Set rng = nm.RefersToRange
            On Error GoTo ErrorHandler

            If Not rng Is Nothing Then
                If rng.Cells.count = 1 And rng.row = rowNum Then
                    colNum = rng.Column
                    colLetter = Split(Cells(1, colNum).Address, "$")(1)

                    ' Strip tab name from named range
                    localName = Replace(nm.Name, Chr(39) & Chr(39), "'")
                    localName = Replace(localName, "'" & ws.Name & "'!", "")
                    localName = Replace(localName, ws.Name & "!", "")

                    innerNumDict(localName) = colNum
                    innerLetDict(localName) = colLetter

                    count = count + 1
                Else
                End If
            End If
        Next nm


        
        ' Only add non-empty dictionaries to NumDict and LetDict
        If count > 0 Then
            If NumDict.Exists(ws.CodeName) Then
                NumDict(ws.CodeName).RemoveAll
                LetDict(ws.CodeName).RemoveAll
            End If
            NumDict.Add key:=ws.CodeName, item:=innerNumDict ' Correct assignment
            LetDict.Add key:=ws.CodeName, item:=innerLetDict ' Correct assignment
            initializedCount = initializedCount + 1
        End If
NextSheet:
    Next wsVar
    
    If initializedCount = 0 Then
        MsgBox "Error: No valid sheets were initialized.", vbExclamation
    End If
    
    Exit Sub
ErrorHandler:
    MsgBox "Error " & Err.Number & ": " & Err.Description & vbCrLf & _
           "In InitializeColumnDictionaries, processing sheet: " & IIf(ws Is Nothing, "Unknown", ws.CodeName) & ", row: " & rowNum, vbCritical
End Sub

Sub WriteDictionaryToSheet()
    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    ' Check if dictionaries are initialized
    If NumDict Is Nothing Or LetDict Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "Error: Dictionaries are not initialized. Run InitializeColumnDictionaries first.", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Define output worksheet (create new or use existing)
    Dim outputWs As Worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set outputWs = ThisWorkbook.worksheets("DictionaryOutput")
    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    If outputWs Is Nothing Then
        Set outputWs = ThisWorkbook.worksheets.Add
        outputWs.Name = "DictionaryOutput"
    Else
        ' Clear existing content
        outputWs.Cells.Clear
    End If
    
    ' Write headers
    With outputWs
        .Cells(1, 1).Value = "Sheet CodeName"
        .Cells(1, 2).Value = "Named Range"
        .Cells(1, 3).Value = "Column Number"
        .Cells(1, 4).Value = "Column Letter"
    End With
    
    ' Initialize row counter for output
    Dim row As Long
    row = 2 ' Start writing data from row 2
    
    ' Iterate through outer dictionaries
    Dim sheetCodeName As Variant
    Dim innerNumDict As Object
    Dim innerLetDict As Object
    Dim namedRange As Variant
    
    For Each sheetCodeName In NumDict.Keys
        ' Get inner dictionaries
        Set innerNumDict = NumDict(sheetCodeName)
        Set innerLetDict = LetDict(sheetCodeName)
        
        ' Iterate through named ranges in inner dictionaries
        For Each namedRange In innerNumDict.Keys
            With outputWs
                .Cells(row, 1).Value = sheetCodeName
                .Cells(row, 2).Value = namedRange
                .Cells(row, 3).Value = innerNumDict(namedRange)
                .Cells(row, 4).Value = innerLetDict(namedRange)
            End With
            row = row + 1
        Next namedRange
    Next sheetCodeName
    
    ' AutoFit columns for better readability
    outputWs.Columns("A:D").AutoFit
    
    MsgBox "Dictionary values have been written to " & outputWs.Name & ".", vbInformation
    Exit Sub

ErrorHandler:
    MsgBox "Error " & Err.Number & ": " & Err.Description & vbCrLf & _
           "In WriteDictionaryToSheet", vbCritical
End Sub



Sub DeleteBrokenNamedRangesWithCOLinJobsGAAP()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim nm As Name
    Dim nameToCheck As String
    
    ' Try to get the "Jobs-GAAP" worksheet
    On Error Resume Next
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Jobs-Ops")
    On Error GoTo 0
    
    ' Check if worksheet exists
    If ws Is Nothing Then
        MsgBox "Worksheet 'Jobs-GAAP' not found.", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Loop through named ranges scoped to the "Jobs-GAAP" worksheet
    For Each nm In ws.Names
        ' Get the name to check
        nameToCheck = nm.Name
        ' Remove 'Jobs-GAAP'! prefix if present
        If InStr(1, nameToCheck, "'Jobs-GAAP'!") = 1 Then
            nameToCheck = Mid(nameToCheck, Len("'Jobs-GAAP'!") + 1)
        End If
        
        ' Diagnostic output to verify values
        Debug.Print "Name: " & nm.Name & ", RefersTo: " & nm.RefersTo & ", nameToCheck: " & nameToCheck
        
        ' Check if the name starts with "COL" (case-insensitive)
        If UCase(Left(nameToCheck, 3)) = "COL" Then
            ' Check if RefersTo contains "#REF!"
            If InStr(1, nm.RefersTo, "#REF!") > 0 Then
                nm.Delete
'                Debug.Print "Deleted broken named range: " & nm.Name & " in 'Jobs-GAAP'"
            End If
        End If
    Next nm
    
    MsgBox "Completed deleting named ranges starting with 'COL' with '#REF!' in 'Jobs-GAAP' scope.", vbInformation
End Sub

Public Sub GetSecurity(User As String)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

'Declare variables'
Dim cnn As ADODB.Connection
Dim cmd As ADODB.Command
Dim DataSQL As String
Dim Datars As ADODB.Recordset
Set cnn = New ADODB.Connection
Set cmd = New ADODB.Command
Set Datars = New ADODB.Recordset
Dim i As Integer
Dim intTotalElements As Integer
Dim intCount As Integer
Dim RoleName As String
Dim RetMsg As String
Dim Companies As String

Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = ""
Sheet2.Range("Companies").Value = ""
Sheet2.Range("Departments").Value = ""

' Open Connection
' If username and password are blank on settings tab use integrated windows user and password for sql query
If CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPPassword").Value) = "" Or CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPUsername").Value) = "" Then
    cnn.connectionString = "Provider=SQLOLEDB.1;Integrated Security=SSPI;Persist Security Info=True;Initial Catalog=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPDBName").Value) & ";Data Source=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPServerName").Value) & ";Use Procedure for Prepare=1;Auto Translate=True;Packet Size=4096;Use Encryption for Data=False;Tag with column collation when possible=False;"
Else
    cnn.connectionString = "Provider=SQLOLEDB.1;Password=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPPassword").Value) & ";Persist Security Info=True;User ID=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPUsername").Value) & ";Initial Catalog=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPDBName").Value) & ";Data Source=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPServerName").Value) & ";Use Procedure for Prepare=1;Auto Translate=True;Packet Size=4096;Workstation ID=MROBERTS;Use Encryption for Data=False;Tag with column collation when possible=False;"
End If

cnn.CommandTimeout = 5
cnn.Open

' GET ROLE

Set cmd = New ADODB.Command
cmd.ActiveConnection = cnn
cmd.CommandType = adCmdStoredProc
cmd.CommandText = "pnp.WIPSECGetRole"
cmd.CommandTimeout = 180



Set cmdUser = cmd.CreateParameter("@user", adVarChar, adParamInput, 30, User)
cmd.Parameters.Append cmdUser
Set cmdRoleName = cmd.CreateParameter("@roleName", adVarChar, adParamOutput, 30)
cmd.Parameters.Append cmdRoleName
Set cmdRetMsg = cmd.CreateParameter("@RetMsg", adVarChar, adParamOutput, 30)
cmd.Parameters.Append cmdRetMsg

cmd.Execute

RoleName = cmd.Parameters("@roleName").Value
RetMsg = cmd.Parameters("@RetMsg").Value

If RetMsg <> "" Then
    MsgBox RetMsg, vbInformation
    GoTo 9998
End If

Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = RoleName

cnn.Close
9998:
GoTo 9999
errexit:
cnn.Close
If Datars.State <> 0 Then
    Datars.Close
End If
MsgBox "There was an error in the GetSecurity Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly

9999: End Sub


Public Sub GetDept(User As String, Company As Integer)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

Application.ScreenUpdating = False

'Declare variables'
Dim cnn As ADODB.Connection
Dim cmd As ADODB.Command
Dim DataSQL As String
Dim Datars As ADODB.Recordset
Set cnn = New ADODB.Connection
Set cmd = New ADODB.Command
Set Datars = New ADODB.Recordset
Dim i As Integer
Dim intTotalElements As Integer
Dim intCount As Integer
Dim Departments As String

Dim RetMsg As String

Sheet2.Range("Departments").Value = ""

' Open Connection
' If username and password are blank on settings tab use integrated windows user and password for sql query
If CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPPassword").Value) = "" Or CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPUsername").Value) = "" Then
    cnn.connectionString = "Provider=SQLOLEDB.1;Integrated Security=SSPI;Persist Security Info=True;Initial Catalog=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPDBName").Value) & ";Data Source=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPServerName").Value) & ";Use Procedure for Prepare=1;Auto Translate=True;Packet Size=4096;Use Encryption for Data=False;Tag with column collation when possible=False;"
Else
    cnn.connectionString = "Provider=SQLOLEDB.1;Password=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPPassword").Value) & ";Persist Security Info=True;User ID=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPUsername").Value) & ";Initial Catalog=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPDBName").Value) & ";Data Source=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPServerName").Value) & ";Use Procedure for Prepare=1;Auto Translate=True;Packet Size=4096;Workstation ID=MROBERTS;Use Encryption for Data=False;Tag with column collation when possible=False;"
End If

cmd.Execute

'Departments = cmd.Parameters("@departments").Value
RetMsg = cmd.Parameters("@RetMsg").Value

cnn.Close

End Sub

VBA MACRO Sheet16.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet16'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Private Sub Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick(ByVal Target As Range, Cancel As Boolean)
    
If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then
    
    'ProtectUnProtect ("Off")
    Me.Unprotect "password"
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    
    ' JV JTD Earned Revenue
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Range("JVJTDEarnedRev")) = "Yes" Then
        
        Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
        
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) <> "=" Then
        
            With Selection.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
            
            Target.Formula = "=IF(" & COLLETJVOvrCostProj & Target.row & "<>0,IF((" & COLLETJVGJTDCost & Target.row _
            & "/" & COLLETJVOvrCostProj & Target.row & ")>0.1,(" & COLJVGJTDCost & Target.row & "/" & COLJVOvrCostProj & Target.row & ")*" & COLJVOvrRevProj & Target.row & ",0),0)"
            Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER & Target.row).Value = "R"
            'Me.Range("AR" & Target.row).Value = 0
        
        Else
        
            If Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER2 & Target.row).Value <> 0 Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER2 & Target.row).Value
                Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = ""
                Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            End If
        
        End If
        
      
    End If
    
    ' Ops JTD Earned Revenue
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Range("OpsJTDEarnedRev")) = "Yes" Then
        
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) <> "=" Then
        
            Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
            
            With Selection.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
            '
            Target.Formula = "=IF(AND(" & COLLETJVOJTDPctComp & Target.row & "<>""," & COLLETJVOvrRevProj & Target.row & "<> "")," & COLLETJVOJTDPctComp & Target.row & "*" & COLLETJVOvrRevProj & Target.row & ",0)"
            Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
            
        Else
            
            If Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER2 & Target.row).Value <> 0 Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER2 & Target.row).Value
                Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = ""
                Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            End If
          
        End If
    End If
    
    ' Ops JTD Cost
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Range("OpsJTDCost")) = "Yes" Then
        
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) <> "=" Then
        
            Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
            
            With Selection.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
            '
            Target.Formula = "=" & COLLETJVGJTDCost & Target.row
            Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDCost & Target.row).Value = "T"
        
        Else
            
            If Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDCost2 & Target.row).Value <> 0 Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range("BE" & Target.row).Value
                Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = ""
                Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDCost & Target.row).Value = "T"
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            End If
          
        End If
        
    End If
    
    
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
    Application.EnableEvents = True

Else
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input!", vbInformation
End If
End Sub


Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
'On Error GoTo errExit
    Me.Unprotect "password"
    Application.EnableEvents = False



If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then

    
    ' Final Approval Yes Button
    If Sheet7.Shapes("Option Button 12").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
    
        If Target.row >= 9 And Target.row <= 40 And Target.Column < 47 Then
                
            If Me.Range("A" & Target.row).Value <> "" Then
                
                ' ACCT - Final Approval (No)
                If Sheet7.Shapes("Option Button 12").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
                    
                    Sheet2.Unprotect "password"
                    Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
                            
                End If
                
                ' JV JTD Earned Revenue
                If Target.Column = COLJVGJTDEarnedRev Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                ' Ops JTD Earned Revenue
                If Target.Column = 17 Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                ' Ops JTD Cost
                If Target.Column = 18 Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDCost & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                               
                
                ' Other Columns
                If Target.Column = COLJVCurContAmt Or Target.Column = COLJVOvrRevProj Or Target.Column = COLJVOvrCostProj _
                Or Target.Column = COLJVCompDate Or Target.Column = COLJVOJTDBonusProfit Or Target.Column = COLJVGDist _
                Or Target.Column = COLJVBILLBillings Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                End If
                
                
                
            
           End If
            
        End If
     
    
        
    Else
    
        MsgBox "Month has Been Final Approved", vbInformation, "Contact Accounting"
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        Application.Undo
        Application.EnableEvents = True
    
    
    End If
    
    
Else
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input", vbInformation
    Application.EnableEvents = True

End If


    
GoTo 999
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an automation error")

999:
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True




End Sub

Public Sub ClearForm(sh As Worksheet)
'Application.ScreenUpdating = False

If sh.CodeName = "Sheet11" Then

    With sh.Range("ExecOvrRevAdj").Interior
        .Pattern = xlSolid
        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .Color = 65535
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
    End With
    
    With sh.Range("ExecOvrCostAdj").Interior
        .Pattern = xlSolid
        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .Color = 65535
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
    End With
    
    With sh.Range("ExecOvrBonusAdj").Interior
        .Pattern = xlSolid
        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .Color = 65535
        .TintAndShade = 0
        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
    End With
End If

 sh.Range("SummaryData").ClearComments
 sh.Range("SummaryData").ClearContents


With sh.Range("Done").Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With

With sh.Range("Done").Borders(xlEdgeTop)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("Done").Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("Done").Borders(xlEdgeRight)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("Done").Borders(xlInsideHorizontal)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = xlAutomatic
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With


On Error Resume Next
With sh.Range("DoneGAAP").Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("DoneGAAP").Borders(xlEdgeTop)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("DoneGAAP").Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("DoneGAAP").Borders(xlEdgeRight)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With
With sh.Range("DoneGAAP").Borders(xlInsideHorizontal)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = xlAutomatic
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlThin
End With



 sh.Range("NotesCost").WrapText = False
 sh.Range("NotesRev").WrapText = False
 sh.Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).Hidden = True
 sh.Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).Hidden = True
 If sh.CodeName = "Sheet11" Then
    sh.Range("Done").ClearContent
 End If
 
 sh.Range("SummaryDataInput").ClearContents
 sh.Range("SummaryDataInput").ClearComments
 sh.Range("SummaryData").Font.Bold = False
 sh.Range("CalcCells").ClearContents
 sh.Range("CalcCells").Font.Bold = False
 sh.Activate


'Reset formulas
 sh.Range("Formulas").Copy
 sh.Range("SummaryDataInput").PasteSpecial Paste:=xlPasteFormulas, Operation:=xlNone, _
    SkipBlanks:=False, Transpose:=False
    

 sh.Range("SummaryDataInput").Font.Bold = False

 sh.Range("Done").Font.Bold = True
 sh.Range("DoneGAAP").Font.Bold = True

Sheet2.Range("Sent").Value = "FALSE"
 sh.Range("B7").Select

End Sub

Public Sub SetColWidth(sh As Worksheet)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

Application.ScreenUpdating = False

Dim Dollars As Integer
Dim SP As Integer
Dim Note As Integer
Dim Profit As Integer
Dollars = 14
SP = 2
Note = 2
Profit = 13

'Ops
If sh.CodeName = "Sheet11" Then
    With sh
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfit")).ColumnWidth = 4
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).ColumnWidth = 4
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLAPYBonusProfit")).ColumnWidth = 4
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCYBonusProfit")).ColumnWidth = 4
    End With
End If

'GAAP
If sh.CodeName = "Sheet12" Then
    With sh
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLGAAPDone")).ColumnWidth = 4
    End With
End If



 ' ALL Sheets
 
 With sh
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJobNumber")).ColumnWidth = 9
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJobDesc")).ColumnWidth = 60
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLPrjMngr")).ColumnWidth = 17
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCurConAmt")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLPMProjRev")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLDone")).ColumnWidth = 4
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProj")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).ColumnWidth = Note
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLPMProjCost")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProj")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).ColumnWidth = Note
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLProjProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLPriorProjProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLChgProjProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCompDate")).ColumnWidth = 11
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLSP1")).ColumnWidth = SP
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDPctComp")).ColumnWidth = 9
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDEarnedRev")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDCost")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDPriorProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDChgProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLSP2")).ColumnWidth = SP
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLAPYPctComp")).ColumnWidth = 11
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLAPYRev")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLAPYCost")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLAPYCalcProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLSP3")).ColumnWidth = SP
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCYRev")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCYCost")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCYCalcProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLSP4")).ColumnWidth = SP
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLBRev")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLBCost")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLBProfit")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLSP5")).ColumnWidth = SP
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLBILLBillings")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLBILLRevExBill")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
    .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLBILLBillExRev")).ColumnWidth = Dollars
End With






If sh.CodeName = "Sheet11" Then
    With sh
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).ColumnWidth = Note
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLAPYBonusProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLCYBonusProfit")).ColumnWidth = Profit
    End With

If sh.CodeName = "Sheet12" Then
    With sh
        .Columns(LetDict(sh.CodeName)("COLGAAPDone")).ColumnWidth = 4
    End With
