VBA MACRO Sheet11.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet11'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 


Private Sub Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick(ByVal Target As Range, Cancel As Boolean)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    GoTo 9999:
End If

Cancel = True
Me.Unprotect "password"
Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.EnableEvents = False

If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If

' JTD Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("JTDHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("JTDPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDChgProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDChgProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("JTDHeading").Select
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "-"
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDChgProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Select
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "+"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If


' APY Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("APYHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("APYPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYBonusProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYBonusProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("APYHeading").Select
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYBonusProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Select
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "+"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If


' CY Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("CYHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("CYPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYBonusProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYBonusProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("CYHeading").Select
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "-"
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYBonusProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Select
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "+"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If

' B Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("BHeading").Select
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "-"
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("BPlus").Select
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "+"
    
    End If
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If



' ALL Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("ALLPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+" Then
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDPriorProfit") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBILLBillExRev")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "-"
    Else
    
        Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDPriorProfit") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDChgProfit")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLAPYBonusProfit")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCYBonusProfit")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBProfit")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBILLBillings") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLBILLBillExRev")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+"
    
    
    End If
        Me.Range("JTDHeading").Select
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If

' Bonus Profit Notes
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BonusProfitNotesShow")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BonusProfitNotes")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Hidden = False Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Me.Range("BonusProfitNotes").WrapText = False
        Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).Select
        If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Value <> "" Then
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow).Value")) = "+"
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).Font.Bold = True
        End If
        
    Else
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).EntireColumn.Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).ColumnWidth = 50
        Me.Cells(Target.row, LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Select
        If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Value <> "" Then
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).Value = "+"
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).Font.Bold = True
        Else
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotesShow")).Value = ""
        End If
        
        With Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes"))
            .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
            .WrapText = True
        End With
        
    End If
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If


' Revenue Notes
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("NotesRevShow")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("NotesRev")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).Hidden = False Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Me.Range("NotesRev").WrapText = False
        Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).Select
        If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).Value <> "" Then
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).Value = "+"
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).Font.Bold = True
        End If
        
    Else
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).EntireColumn.Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).ColumnWidth = 50
        Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).Select
        If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes")).Value <> "" Then
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).Value = "+"
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).Font.Bold = True
        Else
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes2")).Value = ""
        End If
        
        With Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes"))
            .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
            .WrapText = True
        End With
        
    End If
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If


' Cost Notes
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("NotesCostShow")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("NotesCost")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).Hidden = False Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).EntireColumn.Hidden = True
        Me.Range("NotesCost").WrapText = False
        Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).Select
        If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).Value <> "" Then
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).Value = "+"
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).Font.Bold = True
        End If
        
    Else
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).EntireColumn.Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).ColumnWidth = 50
        Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).Select
        If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes")).Value <> "" Then
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).Value = "+"
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).Font.Bold = True
        Else
            Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes2")).Value = ""
        End If
        With Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes"))
            .VerticalAlignment = xlTop
            .WrapText = True
        End With
        
    End If
    Application.EnableEvents = True

GoTo 99
End If

' Closed Month
If Sheet2.Range("LastClosedMth").Value <= Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Value And Sheet2.Range("CheckClosedMonth").Value = "Y" _
    Or Sheet2.Range("LastClosedMth").Value = "" Then
    MsgBox "Cannot Update Closed Month", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If



' Not Ready For Ops
If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value <> "Y" Then
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input!", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If
    

' Done Heading
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("DoneHeading")) = "Yes" Then
    If Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        Application.ScreenUpdating = Fales
        Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
        
        If Sheet2.Range("InitAppr").Value <> "Y" And Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value <> "Y" Then
        
            If MsgBox("    This will toggle all Contracts Done Or Not " & vbCrLf & "       Done that are shown on this page." & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
            "                           Continue?", vbYesNo) = vbYes Then
                If Sheet2.Range("CompleteAll").Value = True Then
                    Call UpdateAllRows(Me, "N")
                    Sheet2.Range("CompleteAll").Value = False
                Else
                
                    Call UpdateAllRows(Me, "Y")
                    Sheet2.Range("CompleteAll").Value = True
                End If
                
                
                
            
            End If
            
        Else
        
            MsgBox "You Need to Un-Approve Before you can take this action", vbInformation
        
        End If
        
        Application.EnableEvents = True
        Application.ScreenUpdating = True
        Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
    Else
    
        MsgBox "Cannot Update - Has been Final Approved For Ops", vbInformation
    
    End If
Sheet11.Activate
GoTo 99
End If
    
    
    
    
' Done
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Done")) = "Yes" Then
   If Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
        
        If Target.Value = "P" Then
            Target.Value = ""
            'Sheet12.Range(LetDict("Sheet12")("COLDone") & Target.row).Value = ""
            Target.ClearComments
        Else
            Target.Value = "P"
            'Sheet12.Range(LetDict("Sheet12")("COLDone") & Target.row).Value = "P"
        End If
        
        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZUserName") & Target.row).Value = Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value
        
        UpdateRow Target.row, Me
        
        
        
        ' Set Border to Thin
        With Target.Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
            .LineStyle = xlContinuous
            .ColorIndex = 0
            .TintAndShade = 0
            .Weight = xlThin
        End With
        With Target.Borders(xlEdgeTop)
            .LineStyle = xlContinuous
            .ColorIndex = 0
            .TintAndShade = 0
            .Weight = xlThin
        End With
        With Target.Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
            .LineStyle = xlContinuous
            .ColorIndex = 0
            .TintAndShade = 0
            .Weight = xlThin
        End With
        With Target.Borders(xlEdgeRight)
            .LineStyle = xlContinuous
            .ColorIndex = 0
            .TintAndShade = 0
            .Weight = xlThin
        End With
    
        
        Application.EnableEvents = True
        Application.ScreenUpdating = True
        Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
        
    Else

        MsgBox "Cannot Update - Has been Final Approved For Ops", vbInformation

    End If
GoTo 99
    
End If
    
' Close
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Close")) = "Yes" Then
        
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.ScreenUpdating = Fales
    Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
    
    If Target.Value = "C" Then
        Target.Value = ""
        Target.ClearComments
    Else
        Target.Value = "C"
        With Target
            .AddComment.Text Text:="Closed By = " & CStr(Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value)
            .Comment.Shape.AutoShapeType = msoShapeRoundedRectangle
            .Comment.Shape.TextFrame.Characters.Font.Name = "Arial"
            .Comment.Shape.TextFrame.Characters.Font.Size = 10
            .Comment.Shape.Height = 25
            .Comment.Shape.Width = 125
        End With
    End If
    
    Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
    Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZUserName") & Target.row).Value = Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value
    
    UpdateRow Target.row, Me
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
    
GoTo 99
End If



' Revenue
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("ExecOvrRevAdj")) = "Yes" Then
    
    ' GAAP View On
    If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn And Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WIPAccounting" Then
        
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) = "=" Or Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Value Then
            
            If Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Value Or Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Value = "" Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRev") & Target.row).Value
                
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOR") & Target.row).Value = ""
                If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRev") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True Then
                    ' Orange
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                Else
                
                    If Target.Value = Target.Offset(0, -2).Value Then
                        ' Yellow
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .Color = 65535
                            .TintAndShade = 0
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                    
                    Else
                        
                        If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOR") & Target.row).Value = "T" Then
                            ' Orange
                            With Target.Interior
                                .Pattern = xlSolid
                                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                                .Color = 49407
                                .TintAndShade = 0
                                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                            End With
                        Else
                            ' Light Red
                            With Target.Interior
                                .Pattern = xlSolid
                                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                                .ThemeColor = xlThemeColorAccent2
                                .TintAndShade = 0.399975585192419
                                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                            End With
                        
                        
                        End If
                    
                    End If
                
                End If
            
            Else
                Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Value
            
                ' Orange
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            
            End If
        
        Else
            Target.Formula = "=" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLPMProjRev") & Target.row
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOR") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProj") & Target.row).Value
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = False
            
            ' Yellow
            With Target.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
        
        
        End If
    
    Else
    ' OPs View
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) = "=" Or Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value Then
            
            If Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value Or Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value = "" Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range(COLZOPsRev & Target.row).Value
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRChg") & Target.row).Value = ""
                
                If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRev") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True Then
                    ' Orange
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                Else
                
                    If Target.Value = Target.Offset(0, -2).Value Then
                        ' Yellow
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .Color = 65535
                            .TintAndShade = 0
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                    
                    Else
                        
                        If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRChg") & Target.row).Value = "T" Then
                            ' Orange
                            With Target.Interior
                                .Pattern = xlSolid
                                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                                .Color = 49407
                                .TintAndShade = 0
                                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                            End With
                        Else
                            ' Light Red
                            With Target.Interior
                                .Pattern = xlSolid
                                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                                .ThemeColor = xlThemeColorAccent2
                                .TintAndShade = 0.399975585192419
                                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                            End With
                        
                        
                        End If
                    
                    End If
                
                End If
            
            Else
                Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value
            
                ' Orange
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            
            End If
        
        Else
            Target.Formula = "=" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLPMProjRev") & Target.row
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value = Me.Range(COLOvrRevProj & Target.row).Value
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = False
            ' Yellow
            With Target.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
        
        
        End If
    
    End If
  
End If


' Exec Overide Cost
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("ExecOvrCostAdj")) = "Yes" Then
    
    ' OPs View
    If Left(Target.Formula, 1) = "=" Or Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value Then
        
        ' If
        If Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value Or _
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value = "" Then
            
            Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCost") & Target.row).Value
            
            If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCost") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True Then
                ' Orange
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
                
            Else
            
                If Target.Value = Target.Offset(0, -1).Value Then
                    ' Yellow
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 65535
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                
                Else
                    
                    If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCChg") & Target.row).Value = "T" Then
                        ' Orange
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .Color = 49407
                            .TintAndShade = 0
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                    Else
                        ' Light Red
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .ThemeColor = xlThemeColorAccent2
                            .TintAndShade = 0.399975585192419
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                    
                    
                    End If
                
                End If
            
            End If
        
        Else
            Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value
                        
            ' Orange
            With Target.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 49407
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
        
        End If
    
    Else
        Target.Formula = "=" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLPMProjCost") & Target.row
        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProj") & Target.row).Value
        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = False
        
        ' Yellow
        With Target.Interior
            .Pattern = xlSolid
            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
            .Color = 65535
            .TintAndShade = 0
            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
        End With
    
    
    End If
    
  
End If

99:
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = True Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If


GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an error in the Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
9999:

End Sub

Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    GoTo 9999:
End If
Application.EnableEvents = False


If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If


Dim CurrentColumnCount As Long

' Get the current number of columns
CurrentColumnCount = Me.Columns.count

' Check if the number of columns has increased
If CurrentColumnCount > LastColumnCount Or IsEmpty(LastColumnCount) = True Then
    LastColumnCount = CurrentColumnCount

End If

' Already Approved
If (Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WIPLevel1" Or Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WIPLevel2") And Sheet2.Range("InitAppr").Value = "Y" Then
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Initial Approval must be set to No before changes can be made", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If

' Marked Ops Done
If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDone")).Value = "P" And Sheet2.Range("GAAPView").Value = "N" Then
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Uncheck the Done Checkbox to make changes", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If





' Done, GAAP Done, Close
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Done")) = "Yes" _
    Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("Close")) = "Yes" Then
    
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    Application.Undo
    
    MsgBox "Double Click to Change Value", vbInformation
    
    Application.EnableEvents = True

    GoTo 99
End If



If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then

    Dim row As Integer
    
    ' Final Approval Yes Button
    If Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
    
        If FindIntersect(Target, Me.Range("SummaryDataInput")) = "Yes" Then
        
            If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJobNumber") & Target.row).Value <> "" Then
                
                If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZContractStatus") & Target.row).Value = 1 Or Sheet2.Range("EditClosedJobs") = True Then
                    
                    If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
                        Me.Unprotect "password"
                    End If
                    
                    ' Revenue
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProj") Then
                        
                       
                        If JTDProfitCheck(Me, CInt(NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProj")), Target.Value, Target.row) = False Then
                            MsgBox "Your Entry has caused JTD Profit to Exceed Profit at Completion", vbInformation
                            Application.Undo
                            GoTo 99
                        End If
                    
                    
     
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
    
                        ' Orange
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .Color = 49407
                            .TintAndShade = 0
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                        GoTo FormatDoneField
                        
                    End If
                    
                    ' Cost
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProj") Then
                    
                        If JTDProfitCheck(Me, CInt(NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProj")), Target.Value, Target.row) = False Then
                            MsgBox "Your Entry has caused JTD Profit to Exceed Profit at Completion", vbInformation
                            Application.Undo
                            GoTo 99
                        End If
    
                        If Target.Value < Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDCost") & Target.row).Value Then
                            MsgBox "Your Entry has Caused % Complete over 100%", vbInformation
                            Application.Undo
                            GoTo 99
                        End If
    
                        
                        
                        
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
                            
                      
                        ' Orange
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .Color = 49407
                            .TintAndShade = 0
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                        GoTo FormatDoneField
                        
                    End If
                    
                    ' Revenue Notes
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrRevProjNotes") Then
                        ' GAAP View On
                        If Me.Shapes("Option Button 23133").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn Then
                            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZJCOR") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZGAAPRevNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Else
                            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsRevNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        End If
                        
                        Target.Offset(0, 1).Value = "+"
                        Target.Offset(0, 1).Font.Bold = True
                        Target.WrapText = True
                        GoTo FormatDoneField
                        
                    End If
                    
                    
                    ' Cost Notes
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLOvrCostProjNotes") Then
                        
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsCostNotes") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        
                        Target.Offset(0, 1).Value = "+"
                        Target.Offset(0, 1).Font.Bold = True
                        Target.WrapText = True
                        GoTo FormatDoneField
                        
                    End If
                    
                    ' Bonus Profit
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfit") Then
                                            
                        If Target.Value > Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLProjProfit") & Target.row).Value Then
                            MsgBox "Profit Not Allowed to be More Than Profit @ Completion", vbInformation
                            Application.Undo
                            GoTo 99
                        End If
                        
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsBonusNew") & Target.row).Value = Target.Value
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZOPsBonusNew") & Target.row).Font.Bold = True
                        ' Orange
                        With Target.Interior
                            .Pattern = xlSolid
                            .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                            .Color = 49407
                            .TintAndShade = 0
                            .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                        End With
                        
                        GoTo FormatDoneField
                    End If
                    
                    
                    ' Bonus Profit Notes
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes") Then
                                            
                        Target.Offset(0, 1).Value = "+"
                        Target.Offset(0, 1).Font.Bold = True
                        Target.WrapText = True
                        Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        
                    End If
                    
                    
                    ' Estimator, PM, Completion Date, COLJTDBonusProfit, COLJTDBonusProfitNotes
                    If Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLEstimator") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLPrjMngr") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLPrjExec") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLCompDate") Or _
                        Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLNotes") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfit") Or Target.Column = NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes") Then
                            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                            ' Add Border to Done field to indicate data needs to be sent back to Vista
                            GoTo FormatDoneField
                        
                    End If
                        
                
                Else
                    
                    Application.Undo
                    
                    MsgBox ("You cannot edit closed Jobs")
                    
                End If
                
            Else
            
                Application.Undo
                MsgBox ("You cannot edit Non-Job Rows")
            
            End If
            
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZUserName") & Target.row).Value = Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value
            
        End If
        
        row = Target.row
        
        
    Else
    
        MsgBox "Month has Been Final Approved", vbInformation, "Contact Accounting"
        Application.EnableEvents = False
        Application.Undo
        Application.EnableEvents = True
    
    
    End If
    
    
Else
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input", vbInformation
    Application.EnableEvents = True

End If

GoTo 9998
FormatDoneField:
' Add Border to Done field to indicate data needs to be sent back to Vista
Dim Col As String

Col = LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDone")

With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With
With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeTop)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With
With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With
With Me.Range(Col & Target.row).Borders(xlEdgeRight)
    .LineStyle = xlContinuous
    .ColorIndex = 0
    .TintAndShade = 0
    .Weight = xlMedium
End With

9998:

    
GoTo 10000
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an error in the Worksheet_Change Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
10000:

Application.ScreenUpdating = True

99:
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

9999:

If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If

End Sub

VBA MACRO UploadData.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/UploadData'

Public Sub SendToVista()
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

Application.ScreenUpdating = False


If IsEmpty(COLJobNo) = True Or COLJobNo = 0 Then
    SetColumns
End If


If Sheet2.Range("LastClosedMth").Value <= Sheet7.Range("Month").Value And Sheet2.Range("CheckClosedMonth").Value = "Y" Then
    MsgBox "Cannot Update Closed Month", vbInformation
    GoTo 99
End If


ProtectUnProtect ("Off")

'Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Sheet7.Activate

8888:


SendToDatabase.Show vbModeless
DoEvents
       
Call CopyWIPDetail

GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an Error in the SendToVista Routine")
9999:

ProtectUnProtect ("On")

Unload SendToDatabase

Application.ScreenUpdating = True
Application.EnableEvents = True

99:

End Sub



Public Sub CopyWIPDetail()
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

If IsEmpty(COLJobNo) = True Or COLJobNo = 0 Then
    SetColumns
End If


Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
Dim MyRow As Range
ProtectUnProtect ("Off")
Sheet8.Range("A4:Z2000").ClearContents


Dim prg As Integer
prg = 4

For Each MyRow In Sheet7.Range("SummaryData").Rows
        
    With MyRow
        
        If MyRow.Cells(1, COLZudChg).Value = "T" Or MyRow.Cells(1, COLZJCOR).Value = "T" Or MyRow.Cells(1, COLZJCOP).Value = "T" Then
        
            If Len(MyRow.Cells(1, COLJobNo).Value) > 0 Then
            
                ' WIPDetail
                Sheet8.Range("A" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(Sheet7.Range("Company").Value)                               ' Co
                Sheet8.Range("B" & CStr(prg)).Value = VBA.Left(CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLJobNo).Value), 2)                 ' Dept
                Sheet8.Range("C" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLJobNo).Value)                              ' Contract
                Sheet8.Range("D" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(Sheet7.Range("Month").Value)                                 ' Month
                If CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZJCOR).Value) = "T" Then
                    Sheet8.Range("E" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPRevNew).Value                          ' GAAPRev
                    
                    If MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPRevNew).Font.Bold = True Then
                        Sheet8.Range("H" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"
                    Else
                        Sheet8.Range("H" & CStr(prg)).Value = "N"
                    End If
                    
                Else
                    Sheet8.Range("E" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPRev).Value
                    
                    If MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPRev).Font.Bold = True Then
                        Sheet8.Range("H" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"                                                       ' GAAP Rev Plugged
                    Else
                        Sheet8.Range("H" & CStr(prg)).Value = "N"
                    End If
                End If
                Sheet8.Range("F" & CStr(prg)).Value = 0                                                                 ' GAAP Other Rev
                Sheet8.Range("G" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPRevNotes).Value)                      ' GAAP RevNotes
                If CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZJCOP).Value) = "T" Then
                    Sheet8.Range("I" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPCostNew).Value                         ' GAAP Cost
                    Sheet8.Range("L" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"                                                           ' GAAP Cost Plugged
                Else
                    If MyRow.Cells(1, COLOvrCostProj).Value > 0 Then
                        Sheet8.Range("I" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLOvrCostProj).Value
                    Else
                        Sheet8.Range("I" & CStr(prg)).Value = 0
                    End If
                    
                    If MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPCost).Font.Bold = True Then
                        Sheet8.Range("L" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"
                    Else
                        Sheet8.Range("L" & CStr(prg)).Value = "N"
                    End If
                    
                End If
                
                Sheet8.Range("J" & CStr(prg)).Value = 0                                                                 ' GAAP Other Cost
                Sheet8.Range("K" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZGAAPCostNotes).Value)                     ' GAAP Cost Notes
                
                If CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLCompDate).Value) <> "" Then
                    Sheet8.Range("M" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLCompDate).Value)                       ' Comp Date
                End If
                
                If CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRChg).Value) = "T" And MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRevNew).Value <> 0 Then      'Op's Rev
                    Sheet8.Range("N" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRevNew).Value
                Else
                    Sheet8.Range("N" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRev).Value
                End If
                
                If CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsCChg).Value) = "T" Or MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsCost).Font.Bold = True Then   ' Op's Cost
                    Sheet8.Range("O" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPSCostNew).Value
                Else
                    Sheet8.Range("O" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsCost).Value
                End If
                
                Sheet8.Range("P" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLEstimator).Value)                          ' Estimator
                Sheet8.Range("Q" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLPrjMngr).Value)                            ' PM
                Sheet8.Range("R" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRevNotes).Value)                       ' Op's Rev Notes
                Sheet8.Range("S" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsCostNotes).Value)                      ' Op's Cost Notes
                Sheet8.Range("T" & CStr(prg)).Value = CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLZUserName).Value)                          ' UserName
                
                If CStr(MyRow.Cells(1, COLDone).Value) = "P" Then                                                       ' Completed
                    Sheet8.Range("U" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"
                Else
                    Sheet8.Range("U" & CStr(prg)).Value = "N"
                End If
                
                If (MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRev).Font.Bold = True Or MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRevNew).Value <> 0) And _
                    MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsRevNew).Value <> MyRow.Cells(1, COLPMProjRev).Value Then                      ' Op's Rev Plug
                        Sheet8.Range("V" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"
                Else
                        Sheet8.Range("V" & CStr(prg)).Value = "N"
                End If
                
                
                
                
                If (MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPsCost).Font.Bold = True Or MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPSCostNew).Value <> 0) And _
                    MyRow.Cells(1, COLZOPSCostNew).Value <> MyRow.Cells(1, COLPMProjCost).Value Then                   ' Op's Cost Plug
                        Sheet8.Range("W" & CStr(prg)).Value = "Y"
                Else
                        Sheet8.Range("W" & CStr(prg)).Value = "N"
                End If
                
                Sheet8.Range("X" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLJTDBonusProfit).Value                           ' BonusProfit
                Sheet8.Range("Y" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLJTDBonusProfitNotes).Value                      ' BonusProfitNotes
                Sheet8.Range("Z" & CStr(prg)).Value = MyRow.Cells(1, COLZBatchSeq).Value                                ' BatchSeq
                
                HasUDData = True
                
                prg = prg + 1
            
            End If
            
        End If

123:

    End With

Next MyRow


Dim pauseTime As Double
pauseTime = 2

If HasUDData = True Then
    SendToDatabase.Label1 = "Sending WIP Details"
    DoEvents
    'Call UploadData("WIPDetail", "budWIPDetail", "LCGRCSUpdatebudWIPDetail")
    Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("0:00:" & pauseTime))
End If


GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an Error in the CopyWIPDetail Routine")
9999:

Sheet2.Range("Sent").Value = True

ProtectUnProtect ("On")
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub


Function GUID$(Optional lowercase As Boolean, Optional parens As Boolean)
    Dim k&, h$
    GUID = Space(36)
    For k = 1 To Len(GUID)
        Randomize
        Select Case k
            Case 9, 14, 19, 24: h = "-"
            Case 15:            h = "4"
            Case 20:            h = Hex(Rnd * 3 + 8)
            Case Else:          h = Hex(Rnd * 15)
        End Select
        Mid$(GUID, k, 1) = h
    Next
    If lowercase Then GUID = LCase$(GUID)
    If parens Then GUID = "{" & GUID & "}"
    GUID = "##RCS" & Replace(GUID, "-", "")
End Function


Public Function CreateColumnList(TabName As String, Def As Boolean)
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

Dim myTab As Excel.Worksheet
Dim myRecord As Range
Dim myField As Range
Dim sOut As String

Dim i As Integer
i = 1
sOut = " ("


For Each myTab In ThisWorkbook.worksheets
    If myTab.Name = TabName Then
         For Each myRecord In myTab.Range("A1:A1")
                With myRecord
                    For Each myField In myTab.Range(.Cells(1), _
                        myTab.Cells(.row, myTab.Columns.count).End(xlToLeft))
                        If Def = True Then
                            sOut = sOut & "[" & Replace(myField.Value, "*", "") & "] " & Replace(myField.Offset(2, 0).Value, "*", "") & ", "
                        Else
                            sOut = sOut & "[" & Replace(myField.Value, "*", "") & "],"
                        End If
                            
                        i = i + 1
                    Next myField
                
                
                End With
            
        Next myRecord
    End If
Next
    
CreateColumnList = Left(sOut, Len(sOut) - 1) & ")"

Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Function


Public Function CreateParamList(TabName As String)
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

Dim myTab As Excel.Worksheet
Dim myRecord As Range
Dim myField As Range
Dim sOut As String

Dim i As Integer
i = 1
sOut = " VALUES ("


For Each myTab In ThisWorkbook.worksheets
    If myTab.Name = TabName Then
         For Each myRecord In myTab.Range("A1:A1")
                With myRecord
                    For Each myField In myTab.Range(.Cells(1), _
                        myTab.Cells(.row, myTab.Columns.count).End(xlToLeft))
                        sOut = sOut & "?,"
                        i = i + 1
                    Next myField
                
                
                End With
            
        Next myRecord
    End If
Next
    

CreateParamList = Left(sOut, Len(sOut) - 1) & ")"


Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Function

Public Function CountCols(TabName As String) As Integer
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

Dim myTab As Excel.Worksheet
Dim myRecord As Range
Dim myField As Range

Dim i As Integer
i = 1

For Each myTab In ThisWorkbook.worksheets
    If myTab.Name = TabName Then
         For Each myRecord In myTab.Range("A1:A1")
                With myRecord
                    For Each myField In myTab.Range(.Cells(1), _
                        myTab.Cells(.row, myTab.Columns.count).End(xlToLeft))
                        
                        i = i + 1
                    Next myField
                
                End With
            
        Next myRecord
    End If
Next

CountCols = i - 1

Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Function

VBA MACRO GetudWIPJV.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/GetudWIPJV'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 

Public Sub GetudWIPJVSub(sh As Worksheet)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

Application.EnableEvents = False
'Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual

sh.Unprotect "password"

Dim Co As String
Dim Dept As String
Dim Mo As String
Dim YrStart As Date
Dim YrEnd As Date
Dim LastGAAPProjContract As Double
Dim PrevProjCost As Double
Dim ExecGAAPContractAdj As Double
Dim ExecGAAPCostAdj As Double
Dim cmd As ADODB.Command
Dim objStrSQL
Dim objStrSQL1
Dim objStrSQL2
Dim ba As Integer

sh.Activate
sh.Range("C11:C35").HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft
sh.Range("B11:B35").HorizontalAlignment = xlLeft

Co = CStr(Sheet17.Range("StartCompany").Value)
Dept = CStr(Sheet17.Range("StartDept").Value)
Mo = CStr(Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Value)

YrStart = "01/01/" & DatePart("yyyy", Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Value)
YrEnd = "12/31/" & (DatePart("yyyy", Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Value) - 1)

Dim row As Range

' Open Connection if not already open
If cnn Is Nothing Then
    Set cnn = New ADODB.Connection
    Dim connectionString As String
    If CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPPassword").Value) = "" Or CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPUsername").Value) = "" Then
        connectionString = "Provider=SQLOLEDB.1;Integrated Security=SSPI;Persist Security Info=True;Initial Catalog=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("WIPDBName").Value) & ";Data Source=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPServerName").Value) & ";Use Procedure for Prepare=1;Auto Translate=True;Packet Size=4096;Use Encryption for Data=False;Tag with column collation when possible=False;"
    Else
        connectionString = "Provider=SQLOLEDB.1;Password=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPPassword").Value) & ";Persist Security Info=True;User ID=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPUsername").Value) & ";Initial Catalog=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("WIPDBName").Value) & ";Data Source=" & CStr(Sheet2.Range("PPServerName").Value) & ";Use Procedure for Prepare=1;Auto Translate=True;Packet Size=4096;Workstation ID=MROBERTS;Use Encryption for Data=False;Tag with column collation when possible=False;"
    End If
    cnn.connectionString = connectionString
    cnn.Open
Else
    If cnn.State <> adStateOpen Then
        cnn.Open
    End If
End If

' Job Status Start and ending row
Dim StartRow As Integer
Dim EndRow As Integer

' Department start and ending rows
Dim DStartRow As Integer
Dim DEndRow As Integer

Dim OpenRowTotal As Integer

' Check if Datars is Nothing or closed, then open it
If Datars Is Nothing Then
    Set Datars = New ADODB.Recordset
    Set cmd = New ADODB.Command
    cmd.ActiveConnection = cnn
    cmd.CommandType = adCmdStoredProc
    cmd.CommandText = "LCGWIPGetDetailJV"
    cmd.CommandTimeout = 180
    
    Set cmdCo = cmd.CreateParameter("@Co", adTinyInt, adParamInput, 1, Co)
    cmd.Parameters.Append cmdCo
    Set cmdMonth = cmd.CreateParameter("@Month", adDate, adParamInput, 0, CDate(Mo))
    cmd.Parameters.Append cmdMonth
    cnn.CursorLocation = adUseClient
    
    Datars.Open cmd.Execute
Else
        Datars.MoveFirst
End If


If Datars.EOF <> True Then

    Datars.MoveLast
    Datars.MoveFirst

    T = Datars.RecordCount
    Dim i As Integer
    Dim r As Integer
    Dim Div As String
    Div = "None"
    Dim Status As Integer
    Status = 0
    r = 1
    StartRow = sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Rows(r).row
    DStartRow = StartRow
    
    Dim OCompleted As String
    Dim GCompleted As String

    For i = 1 To T
    
        
        If Datars.Fields("OCompleted").Value = "Y" Then
            OCompleted = "P"
        Else
            OCompleted = ""
        End If
        
        If Datars.Fields("GCompleted").Value = "Y" Then
            GCompleted = "P"
        Else
            GCompleted = ""
        End If

        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVMMJobNo")) = Datars.Fields("JVJobNum").Value
        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJobNo")) = Datars.Fields("IntJobNum").Value
        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVSupJobNo")) = Datars.Fields("SupJobNumber").Value
        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJobDesc")) = Datars.Fields("JVJobDesc").Value
        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVPartners")) = Datars.Fields("JVPartners").Value
        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVSharePct")) = Datars.Fields("OurJVPct").Value
        sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLZBatchSeq")) = Datars.Fields("BatchSeq").Value
        
        If sh.CodeName = "Sheet14" Then ' Ops
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLDone")) = OCompleted
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVCurContAmt")) = Datars.Fields("OpsContractAmt").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVOvrRevProj")) = Datars.Fields("OpsProjectedRevenue").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj")) = Datars.Fields("OpsProjectedCost").Value
            
            If Datars.Fields("OpsEarnedRev").Value <> 0 Then
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJTDEarnedRev")) = Datars.Fields("OpsEarnedRev").Value
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER2")) = Datars.Fields("OpsEarnedRev").Value
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER")) = "T"
                With sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJTDEarnedRev")).Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            Else
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg")) = 0
            End If
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJTDCost")) = Datars.Fields("OpsJTDCost").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVBILLBillings")) = Datars.Fields("OpsJTDBillings").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev")) = Datars.Fields("PYOpsEarnedRevenue").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCost")) = Datars.Fields("PYOpsPJTDCost").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLZUserName")) = Datars.Fields("OUserName").Value
            For ba = LBound(Datars.Fields("ORowVersion").Value) To UBound(Datars.Fields("ORowVersion").Value)
                hexString = hexString & Right("0" & Hex(Datars.Fields("ORowVersion").Value(ba)), 2)
            Next ba
            
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLZRowVersion")) = hexString
            hexString = ""
        
        Else 'GAAP
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLDone")) = OCompleted
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLDoneGAAP")) = GCompleted
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVCurContAmt")) = Datars.Fields("GAAPContractAmt").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVProjFinalProfit")) = Datars.Fields("GAAPProjectedFinalProfit").Value
            If Datars.Fields("GAAPEarnedRev").Value <> 0 Then
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJTDEarnedRev")) = Datars.Fields("GAAPEarnedRev").Value
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER2")) = Datars.Fields("GAAPEarnedRev").Value
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER")) = "T"
                With sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJTDEarnedRev")).Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
        
            Else
                sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg")) = 0
            End If
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVJTDCost")) = Datars.Fields("GAAPJTDCost").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVBILLBillings")) = Datars.Fields("GAAPJTDBillings").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev")) = Datars.Fields("PYGAAPEarnedRevenue").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCost")) = Datars.Fields("PYGAAPJTDCost").Value
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLZUserName")) = Datars.Fields("GUserName").Value
            For ba = LBound(Datars.Fields("GRowVersion").Value) To UBound(Datars.Fields("GRowVersion").Value)
                hexString = hexString & Right("0" & Hex(Datars.Fields("GRowVersion").Value(ba)), 2)
            Next ba
            
            sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, NumDict(sh.CodeName)("COLZRowVersion")) = hexString
            hexString = ""
        
        End If
        
        Datars.MoveNext
        r = r + 1
    
    Next

End If

If sh.CodeName = "Sheet15" Then
    Datars.Close
    cnn.Close
End If

Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic

GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an error geting Data From Viewpoint")
If Datars.State <> 0 Then
Datars.Close
End If
cnn.Close
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
9999:

If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = True Then
    sh.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If

sh.Range("A1").Select
Application.EnableEvents = True
'Application.ScreenUpdating = True


Sheet17.Activate

End Sub



Public Sub SetTotalsJV(r As Integer, StartRow As Integer, EndRow As Integer, Col As String, sh As Worksheet)

sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, ColLetToNum(Col)).Formula = "=Sum(" & Col & StartRow & ":" & Col & EndRow & ")"
sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, ColLetToNum(Col)).Font.Bold = True

End Sub

Public Sub SetDTotalsJV(r As Integer, StartRow As Integer, EndRow As Integer, Col As String, sh As Worksheet)

sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, ColLetToNum(Col)).Formula = "=Sum(" & Col & StartRow & ":" & Col & EndRow & ")/2"
sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, ColLetToNum(Col)).Font.Bold = True

End Sub



Public Sub SetGrandTotalsJV(r As Integer, OpenRowTotal As Integer, EndRow As Integer, Col As String, sh As Worksheet)

sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, ColLetToNum(Col)).Formula = "=Sum(" & Col & "5" & ":" & Col & EndRow + 1 & ")/4"
' Open Job Totals
sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r - 2, ColLetToNum(Col)).Formula = "=SUMIF(AX5:AX" & EndRow & ",1, " & Col & "5" & ":" & Col & EndRow & ")"

' Closed Job Totals
sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r - 1, ColLetToNum(Col)).Formula = "=SUMIF(AX5:AX" & EndRow & ",2, " & Col & "5" & ":" & Col & EndRow & ")"


sh.Range("SummaryDataJV").Cells(r, ColLetToNum(Col)).Font.Bold = True

End Sub

VBA MACRO FormButtons.bas 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/FormButtons'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Sub RFOYes_Click()
' ACCT - Ready For Ops (Yes)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

If Len(Sheet17.Range("StartCompany").Value) <> 0 And Len(Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Value) <> 0 And Len(Sheet17.Range("StartDept").Value) <> 0 Then

    Select Case Sheet2.Range("Role").Value
    
    
        Case "":
    
    
        Case "WIPAccounting":
        
                Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y"
                Sheet2.Range("SendAppr").Value = "True"
                Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                UpdateApprovals
                
        Case Else:
        
            MsgBox "Only Accounting Can Change This Setting", vbInformation
            ' Set Ready For Ops to No
            Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
        
    End Select

Else
    
    Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
    Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
    MsgBox "Select Company, Month And Division to Create new WIP Month", vbInformation
End If

Sheet17.Activate
Sheet17.Range("StartCompany").Select

GoTo 9999
errexit:
Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
MsgBox "There was an error in the RFOYes_Click Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly

9999:

End Sub


Sub RFONo_Click()
' ACCT - Ready For Ops (No)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WIPAccounting" Then

    If Sheet17.Range("StartCompany").Value <> "" And Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Value <> "" And Sheet17.Range("StartDept").Value <> "" Then
    
        If MsgBox("This will delete all WIP Information for the Company, Month and Divisions Selected.  Are you sure?", vbYesNo) = vbYes Then
        
            Select Case Sheet2.Range("Role").Value
            
                Case "":
            
            
                Case "WIPAccounting":
                    Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                    Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                    Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "N"
                    Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "N"
                    Sheet2.Range("SendAppr").Value = "True"
                    UpdateApprovals
                    ClearWIPDetailTable
                
                
                Case Else:
                
                    MsgBox "Only Accounting Can Change This Setting", vbInformation
                    If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "N" Then
                        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                    
                    Else
                        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                    
                    End If
                    
            End Select
        
        Else
            If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "N" Then
                Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
            
            Else
                Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-es").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            
            End If
        
        End If
    
    Else
        MsgBox "Select Company and Month to Clear Existing Data", vbInformation
    End If


Else

    MsgBox "Only Accounting Can Change this setting", vbInformation
    
    If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "N" Then
        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
    
    Else
        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
        Sheet17.Shapes("RFO-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
    
    End If



End If

GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an error in the RFONo_Click Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
9999:
End Sub


Sub OFANo_Click()
' Final Approval (No)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then
    
    Select Case Sheet2.Range("Role").Value
    
    
        Case "":
        
        Case "WIPLevel2":
    
            ' Set Final Approval to No
            Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
            Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "N"
            Sheet2.Range("SendAppr").Value = "True"
            UpdateApprovals
    
        Case "WIPAccounting":
        
            ' Set Final Approval to No
            Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
            Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "N"
            Sheet2.Range("SendAppr").Value = "True"
            UpdateApprovals
    
    
        Case Else:
        
            MsgBox "Only Final Approvers Can Change This Setting", vbInformation
            Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff

    
    End Select
    
Else

    MsgBox "Period Not Ready for Ops Input", vbOKOnly, "Contact Accounting"
    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOf
    Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "N"

End If

GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an error in the OFANo_Click Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
9999:
Sheet17.Activate

End Sub

    On Error GoTo errexit

                    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn

                    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff

                End If
                
            Case "WIPAccounting":
        
                If CompleteCheck("O", "") = True Then
                    ' Set Final Approval to Yes
                    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                    Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "Y"
                    UpdateApprovals
                Else
                    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
                End If
        
        
            Case Else:
            
                MsgBox "Only Final Approvers Can Change This Setting", vbInformation
                Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
                Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
    
        
        End Select
        
    
    
    
Else

    MsgBox "Period Not Ready for Ops Input", vbInformation, "Contact Accounting"
    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
    Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
    Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "N"

End If

GoTo 9999
errexit:
Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
MsgBox "There was an error in the OFAYes_Click Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
9999:

Sheet17.Activate

End Sub

Sub AFAYes_Click()
' ACCT - Final Approval (Yes)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If

Select Case Sheet2.Range("Role").Value
    Case "":
    Case "WIPAccounting":

        If Sheet2.Range("FinalAppr").Value = "Y" Then
            Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
            Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            Sheet2.Range("AcctAppr").Value = "Y"
            Sheet2.Range("SendAppr").Value = "True"
            
            
            If CompleteCheck("G", "") = True Then
                UpdateApprovals
            End If
            
        Else
        
            MsgBox "Need Ops Approval", vbInformation, "Waiting On Ops Final Approval"
            Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
            Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
        
        End If

    Case Else:
    
        MsgBox "Only Accounting Can Change This Setting", vbInformation

        Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
        Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
        Sheet2.Range("AcctAppr").Value = "N"
        Sheet2.Range("SendAppr").Value = "True"

End Select



GoTo 9999
errexit:
Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-No").ControlFormat.Value = xlOn
Sheet17.Shapes("AFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff
MsgBox "There was an error in the AFAYes_Click Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
9999:

Sheet17.Activate
End Sub




Sub SetJVRolePermissions(sh As Worksheet)


If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value <> "WIPAccounting" Then

    sh.Range("JTDBill").Locked = True
    'Revenue Color
    With sh.Range("JTDBill").Interior
        .Pattern = xlSolid
        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .ThemeColor = xlThemeColorDark2
        .TintAndShade = -0.249977111117893
        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
    End With
    With sh.Range("JTDBillHeading").Interior
        .Pattern = xlSolid
        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
        .ThemeColor = xlThemeColorDark2
        .TintAndShade = -0.249977111117893
        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
    End With

        .Pattern = xlSolid

        .PatternTintAndShade = 0

    With sh.Range("OPCCAHeading").Interior
