VBA MACRO Sheet15.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet15'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
Private Sub Worksheet_BeforeDoubleClick(ByVal Target As Range, Cancel As Boolean)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    GoTo 9999:
End If

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual

If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If

Me.Unprotect "password"

' JTD Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("JTDHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("JTDPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDProfit")).Hidden = False
        'Me.Columns(NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJTDBonusProfitNotes")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("JTDHeading").Select
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Select
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "J T D"
    
    End If
    
    

GoTo 99
End If


' APY Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("APYHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("APYPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("APYHeading").Select
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Select
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "A P Y"
    
    End If
    

GoTo 99
End If


' CY Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("CYHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("CYPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("CYHeading").Select
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Select
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "C Y"
    
    End If
    

GoTo 99
End If

' B Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BHeading")) = "Yes" Or FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("BPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = True Then
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Range("BHeading").Select
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Range("BPlus").Select
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "B L"
    
    End If
    

GoTo 99
End If



' ALL Show Hide
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("ALLPlus")) = "Yes" Then
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    
    If Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+" Then
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = False
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = False
        
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "-"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = ""
    Else
    
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDPctComp") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOJTDProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVAPYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCYCalcProfit")).Hidden = True
        Me.Columns(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBRev") & ":" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVBProfit")).Hidden = True
        
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("ALLPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Value = "+"
        Me.Range("JTDPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "J T D"
        Me.Range("APYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "A P Y"
        Me.Range("CYPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "C Y"
        Me.Range("BPlus").Offset(1, 0).Value = "B L"
    
    
    End If
    Me.Range("JTDHeading").Select

GoTo 99
End If








If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then
    
    'ProtectUnProtect ("Off")
    Me.Unprotect "password"
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    ' Done
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("DoneGAAP")) = "Yes" Then
       If Sheet17.Shapes("OFA-Yes").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
            Application.EnableEvents = False
            Application.ScreenUpdating = Fales
            Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual
            
            If Target.Value = "P" Then
                Target.Value = ""
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDoneGAAP") & Target.row).Value = ""
                Target.ClearComments
            Else
                Target.Value = "P"
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDoneGAAP") & Target.row).Value = "P"
            End If
            
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLZUserName") & Target.row).Value = Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value
            
            UpdateRowJV Target.row, Me
            
            
            
            ' Set Border to Thin
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeLeft)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeTop)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeBottom)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
            With Target.Borders(xlEdgeRight)
                .LineStyle = xlContinuous
                .ColorIndex = 0
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .Weight = xlThin
            End With
        
            
            Application.ScreenUpdating = True
            
        Else
    
            MsgBox "Cannot Update - Has been Final Approved For Ops", vbInformation
    
        End If
    GoTo 99
        
    End If
    
    ' JV JTD Earned Revenue
    If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Range("JVJTDEarnedRevenue")) = "Yes" Then
        
        Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
        
        If Left(Target.Formula, 1) <> "=" Then
        
            With Selection.Interior
                .Pattern = xlSolid
                .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                .Color = 65535
                .TintAndShade = 0
                .PatternTintAndShade = 0
            End With
            
            Target.Formula = "=IF(" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj") & Target.row & "<>0,IF((" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDCost") & Target.row _
            & "/" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj") & Target.row & ")>0.1,(" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVJTDCost") & Target.row & "/" & _
            LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVOvrCostProj") & Target.row & ")*" & LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVCurContAmt") & Target.row & ",0),0)"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg") & Target.row).Value = "T"
            Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER") & Target.row).Value = "R"
    
        Else
    
            If Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER2") & Target.row).Value <> 0 Then
                Target.Value = Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER2") & Target.row).Value
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZudChg") & Target.row).Value = ""
                Me.Range(LetDict(Me.CodeName)("COLJVZJTDER") & Target.row).Value = "T"
                With Target.Interior
                    .Pattern = xlSolid
                    .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                    .Color = 49407
                    .TintAndShade = 0
                    .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                End With
            End If
    
        End If
        
        Target.Select
        Cancel = True
        
    End If
        
      
    If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = True Then
        Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
    End If
       
    

Else
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input!", vbInformation
End If

GoTo 99
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an Error in the Double Click Routine" & Err, vbOKOnly

99:
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic

9999:
End Sub


Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
If Sheet2.Range("Role").Value = "WipViewOnly" Then
    MsgBox "You do not have permission to edit.", vbOKOnly, "View Olny Permission"
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    Application.Undo
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    GoTo 9999:
End If

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False
Application.Calculation = xlCalculationManual

If NumDict Is Nothing Then
    InitializeColumnDictionaries NumDict, LetDict, 1
End If

Me.Unprotect "password"

If Sheet2.Range("ReadyForOpsAppr1").Value = "Y" Then

        ' Marked Ops Done
    If Me.Cells(Target.row, NumDict(Me.CodeName)("COLDoneGAAP")).Value = "P" Then
        Application.Undo
        MsgBox "Uncheck the Done Checkbox to make changes", vbInformation
        GoTo 99
    End If


    
    ' Final Approval Yes Button
    If Sheet7.Shapes("Option Button 12").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
    
        If Target.row >= 9 And Target.row <= 40 And Target.Column < 47 Then
                
            If Me.Range("A" & Target.row).Value <> "" Then
                
                ' ACCT - Final Approval (No)
                If Sheet7.Shapes("Option Button 12").ControlFormat.Value = xlOff Then
                    
                    Sheet2.Unprotect "password"
                    Sheet2.Range("SendJV").Value = "True"
                            
                End If
                
                ' JV JTD Earned Revenue
                If Target.Column = COLJVGJTDEarnedRev Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZGJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                ' Ops JTD Earned Revenue
                If Target.Column = 17 Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDER & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                ' Ops JTD Cost
                If Target.Column = 18 Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZOJTDCost & Target.row).Value = "T"
                    
                    With Target.Interior
                        .Pattern = xlSolid
                        .PatternColorIndex = xlAutomatic
                        .Color = 49407
                        .TintAndShade = 0
                        .PatternTintAndShade = 0
                    End With
                    
                End If
                
                               
                
                ' Other Columns
                If Target.Column = COLJVCurContAmt Or Target.Column = COLJVOvrRevProj Or Target.Column = COLJVOvrCostProj _
                Or Target.Column = COLJVCompDate Or Target.Column = COLJVOJTDBonusProfit Or Target.Column = COLJVGDist _
                Or Target.Column = COLJVBILLBillings Then
                        Me.Range(COLLETJVZudChg & Target.row).Value = "T"
                End If
                
                
                
            
           End If
            
        End If
     
    
        
    Else
    
        MsgBox "Month has Been Final Approved", vbInformation, "Contact Accounting"
        
        Application.Undo
        
    
    
    End If
    
    
Else
    
    Application.Undo
    MsgBox "Period Is Not Ready For Ops Input", vbInformation
    

End If


    
GoTo 99
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an automation error")

99:
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

Application.Calculation = xlCalculationAutomatic
9999:

End Sub

Option Explicit

9999:

Private Sub UserForm_Activate()
Set PRange = ActiveCell

End Sub


Private Sub UserForm_Initialize()
On Error GoTo errexit

Dim intTotalElements As Integer

On Error GoTo 50

'Check if Form 1 list is already in the array
intTotalElements = UBound(Form3Datalist) - LBound(Form3Datalist) + 1
50:

'If not poll the database and fill the array
'If intTotalElements = 0 Then

'Call GetForm3Data(Form3Datalist())

'End If

With Me.ListBox1
    .Clear
    .List = Form3Datalist
End With

GoTo 9999
errexit:

9999:
End Sub

Private Sub SetDataVal()
'On Error GoTo errExit

Application.EnableEvents = False
Application.ScreenUpdating = False

ProtectUnProtect ("Off")

Dim i As Integer

For i = 0 To ListBox1.ListCount - 1
    If ListBox1.Selected(i) = True Then
        Sheet7.Range("BatchId").Value = VBA.Left(ListBox1.Column(0, i), 3)
        Sheet7.Range("DEPT").Value = LTrim(RTrim(VBA.Mid(ListBox1.Column(0, i), 4, 30)))
    End If
Next

GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an Error in the SetDataVal Routine")
9999:

'Call GetDept(Sheet2.Range("UserName2").Value, Sheet7.Range("Company").Value)


Sheet7.Range("Month").Select
ProtectUnProtect ("On")
BatchSelected = True

Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
End Sub

'search function on list box (note .column (0,i) and .column(1,i) fields indicate that both columns A and B are being searched)
Private Sub CommandButton1_Click()
On Error GoTo errexit

Dim strSearch As String
Dim i As Long
Dim iContinueSearch As Integer
Dim Filecount As Variant
 
btnClearAll_Click
TextBox1.Value = ""

 'strSearch = VBA.UCase("*" & TextBox2.Value & "*")

 With Me.ListBox1

 If .ListCount > 0 Then
    For i = 0 To .ListCount - 2
        If .Column(0, i) Like strSearch Then
            .Selected(i) = True
            .ListIndex = i + (.Height / 15)
            iContinueSearch = MsgBox("Find Next?", vbQuestion + vbYesNo)
            If iContinueSearch = vbYes Then
               .Selected(i) = False
            End If
            If iContinueSearch = vbNo Then
                Exit For
            End If
        End If
    Next i
    
 End If
 End With

GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox ("There was an Error in the CommandButton1_Click Routine")
9999:


End Sub

Option Explicit

Private Declare PtrSafe Function FindWindow Lib "user32" Alias "FindWindowA" _
    (ByVal lpClassName As String, ByVal lpWindowName As String) As LongPtr

Private Declare PtrSafe Function MoveWindow Lib "user32" _
    (ByVal hWnd As LongPtr, ByVal x As LongPtr, ByVal y As LongPtr, ByVal nWidth As LongPtr, ByVal nHeight As LongPtr, ByVal bRepaint As LongPtr) As LongPtr

Const MESSAGE_TITLE As String = "My Message Box"

Sub ShowAndMoveMsgBox()
    Dim hWnd As LongPtr
    Dim RetVal As LongPtr
    Dim frm As DataRetrievalStatus
    Set frm = New DataRetrievalStatus
    
    frm.Label1.Caption = "Getting Data......."
    
    
    frm.StartUpPosition = 0
    ' Calculate the position where the UserForm should appear to be centered in Excel
    frm.Left = Application.Left + (0.5 * Application.Width) - (0.5 * frm.Width)
    frm.Top = Application.Top + (0.5 * Application.Height) - (0.5 * frm.Height)
    
    
    
    
    frm.Show vbModeless
    
    

    ' Small delay to ensure the MsgBox has time to appear
    Application.Wait (Now + TimeValue("0:00:01"))

End Sub

VBA MACRO Sheet17.cls 
in file: xl/vbaProject.bin - OLE stream: 'VBA/Sheet17'
- - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 

Private Sub Worksheet_Change(ByVal Target As Range)
If Sheet2.Range("ErrorCtl").Value = True Then
    On Error GoTo errexit
End If
Application.EnableEvents = False


' Company
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("StartCompany")) = "Yes" Then
    
    Application.EnableEvents = False
    ' This checks list of accessable Companies returned during GetSecurity Check on Workbook open
    Sheet17.Range("StartCoName").Value = GetCoName(Target.Value)
    If Sheet17.Range("StartCoName").Value = "" Then
        Target.Value = ""
    End If
    Application.EnableEvents = True
    
    GoTo 99

End If

' Month
If FindIntersect(Range(Target.Address), Me.Range("StartMonth")) = "Yes" Then
    
    If IsValidDateRegex(Target.Value) = True Then
        

        Application.ScreenUpdating = False
        
        Me.Unprotect "password"
        Me.Range("StartDept").Value = ""
        
        If IsDate(Target.Value) Then
            Target.Value = DateSerial(Year(Target.Value), Month(Target.Value), 1)
        End If
        
        ClearForms3
        ' Check status of the GL Month
        GLCheck
        
        Dim NoData As Boolean
        NoData = False
        
        
        
        ' Check if WIPDetail has data
        UseExistingBatch NoData
            
        If NoData = False Then
            GetWipDetail2 Sheet11
            GetWipDetail2 Sheet12
            GetudWIPJVSub Sheet14
            GetudWIPJVSub Sheet15
        End If
        
        Sheet11.Activate
        Sheet11.Range("A2").Select
        Sheet12.Activate
        Sheet12.Range("A2").Select
        Sheet17.Activate
        Sheet17.Range("StartMonth").Select
        
        GoTo 99
        
    Else
        

        MsgBox "Enter a valid date. ", vbOKOnly
        Application.Undo
        Target.Select
        GoTo 99
        
    
    End If

End If


GoTo 9999
errexit:
MsgBox "There was an error in the Worksheet_Change Routine. " & Err, vbOKOnly
9999:
If Sheet2.Range("ProtectSheet").Value = "True" Then
    Me.Protect "password", AllowFormattingColumns:=True, AllowFormattingCells:=True, AllowFormattingRows:=True
End If
Application.ScreenUpdating = True

99:
Application.EnableEvents = True
Application.ScreenUpdating = True


End Sub


Function IsValidDateRegex(inputValue As Variant) As Boolean
    On Error GoTo ErrHandler
    
    ' Check for empty or invalid inputs
    If IsEmpty(inputValue) Or IsNull(inputValue) Or Trim(inputValue) = "" Then
        IsValidDateRegex = False
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Convert input to string
    Dim strInput As String
    strInput = CStr(inputValue)
    
    ' Set up regex for #/#/####, #/#/##, ##/##/####, ##-##-####, #-#-####, #-#-##
    Dim regEx As Object
    Set regEx = CreateObject("VBScript.RegExp")
    With regEx
        .Pattern = "^(0?[1-9]|1[0-2])[-/](0?[1-9]|[12][0-9]|3[01])[-/]([0-9]{2}|[0-9]{4})$"
        .IgnoreCase = True
        .Global = False
    End With
    
    ' Check if input matches the pattern
    If Not regEx.Test(strInput) Then
        IsValidDateRegex = False
        Set regEx = Nothing
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Validate as a true date using IsDate
    If IsDate(strInput) Then
        Dim testDate As Date
        testDate = CDate(strInput)
        ' Ensure year is within Excel's valid range (1900–9999)
        If Year(testDate) >= 1900 And Year(testDate) <= 9999 Then
            IsValidDateRegex = True
        Else
            IsValidDateRegex = False
        End If
    Else
        IsValidDateRegex = False
    End If
    
    Set regEx = Nothing
    Exit Function

ErrHandler:
    IsValidDateRegex = False
    Set regEx = Nothing
End Function

+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
|Type      |Keyword             |Description                                  |
+----------+--------------------+---------------------------------------------+
|AutoExec  |Workbook_Open       |Runs when the Excel Workbook is opened       |
|AutoExec  |Workbook_BeforeClose|Runs when the Excel Workbook is closed       |
|AutoExec  |GetVPData_Click     |Runs when the file is opened and ActiveX     |
|          |                    |objects trigger events                       |
|AutoExec  |TextBox1_Change     |Runs when the file is opened and ActiveX     |
|          |                    |objects trigger events                       |
|Suspicious|Open                |May open a file                              |
|Suspicious|Write               |May write to a file (if combined with Open)  |
|Suspicious|Output              |May write to a file (if combined with Open)  |
|Suspicious|Run                 |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command                                      |
|Suspicious|Create              |May execute file or a system command through |
|          |                    |WMI                                          |
|Suspicious|Command             |May run PowerShell commands                  |
|Suspicious|Call                |May call a DLL using Excel 4 Macros (XLM/XLF)|
|Suspicious|CreateObject        |May create an OLE object                     |
|Suspicious|GetObject           |May get an OLE object with a running instance|
|Suspicious|windows             |May enumerate application windows (if        |
|          |                    |combined with Shell.Application object)      |
|Suspicious|FindWindow          |May enumerate application windows (if        |
|          |                    |combined with Shell.Application object)      |
|Suspicious|Lib                 |May run code from a DLL                      |
|Suspicious|Chr                 |May attempt to obfuscate specific strings    |
|          |                    |(use option --deobf to deobfuscate)          |
|Suspicious|system              |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command on a Mac (if combined with           |
|          |                    |libc.dylib)                                  |
|Suspicious|Exec                |May run an executable file or a system       |
|          |                    |command using Excel 4 Macros (XLM/XLF)       |
